        <div class="shape" style="padding:5.88pt 5.88pt 5.88pt 5.88pt" v:shape="_x0000_s38105">
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
   Arial;language:en-US">
           T
          </span>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;
   font-family:Arial;color:#000099;language:en-US">
           he
          </span>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:#000099;font-weight:bold;
   language:en-US">
           Melorheostosis Association
          </span>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           is a 501(c)(3) not-for-profit organization dedicated to finding the cause, treatments  and cure for melorheostosis.  Our focus is on promoting greater awareness and understanding of this progressive disease and its manifestations through education, research, communication and advocacy efforts on behalf of those affected by it as well as those dedicated to alleviating it. For a full list of our Board of Directors,

     <v:fill color2="white [7]">
     </v:fill>
     <v:stroke color2="white [7]">
      <o:left color="#699 [2]" color2="white [7]" joinstyle="miter" v:ext="view" weight="4.5pt">

     <v:textbox inset="2.88pt,2.88pt,2.88pt,2.88pt" style="mso-column-margin:2mm">
     </v:textbox>
    </v:shape>
    <span style="position:absolute;z-index:545;
 left:903px;top:435px;width:510px;height:522px">
     <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
      <tr>
       <td height="522" style="border:3.0pt solid #669999;vertical-align:
   top" width="510">
        <div class="shape" style="padding:5.88pt 5.88pt 5.88pt 5.88pt" v:shape="_x0000_s38107">
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
   Arial;font-weight:bold;language:en-US">
           Melorheostosis
          </span>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           is a rare and progressive disorder characterized by  hyperostosis (thickening) of the cortical bone.  Melorheostosis affects both bone and soft tissue growth and development.   Melorheostosis can result in severe functional limitation, extensive pain, soft tissue contractures, and limb, hand an/or foot deformity.  The age of diagnosis is typically based on the severity of onset and symptoms.  On x-rays, the appearance of melorheostosis been likened to flowing, melted candle  wax.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
   Arial;language:en-US">
           Note:  Diseases associated with melorheostosis include, osteopoikilosis, osteopathia striata, scleroderma and Buschke-Ollendorff syndrome.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;line-height:75%;text-align:center">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;line-height:75%;color:#000099;font-weight:
   bold;language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;line-height:75%;text-align:center">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;line-height:75%;color:#000099;font-weight:
   bold;language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;line-height:75%;text-align:center">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;line-height:75%;color:#000099;font-weight:
   bold;language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;line-height:75%;text-align:center">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;line-height:75%;color:#000099;font-weight:
   bold;language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;line-height:75%;text-align:center">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;line-height:75%;color:#000099;font-weight:
   bold;language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;text-align:center">
          <a href="default_files/Page741.htm">

   font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;font-weight:bold;language:en-US">

           </span>

          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:#000099;
   font-weight:bold;language:en-US">
           Help the Medical Community Know How Many People are Affected by Melorheostosis
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoNormal">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Arial;
   language:en-US">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
   125%;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           Through the power of the Internet, we have established a community of melorheostosis patients from around the world.  Our isolation as individual patients has ended and we have come together, along with our dedicated Medical Panel, to find answers.  Below are links to maps showing the location of melorheostosis patients who have posted their personal histories on this website.  We will also be adding patients who contact us but do not wish to post their personal history (see instructions below).
          </span>
         </p>

    <span style="position:absolute;z-index:550;
 left:90px;top:4152px;width:1374px;height:342px">
     <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
      <tr>
       <td height="342" style="vertical-align:top" width="1374">
        <div class="shape" style="padding:2.88pt 2.88pt 2.88pt 2.88pt" v:shape="_x0000_s38116">
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
   125%;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           We are hoping even more melorheostosis patients will come forward this year. Please contact us so we can “put you on the map.” You have two options:
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
   125%;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           <span dir="ltr">
           </span>
           1.To post your personal history, go to the “A
          </span>
          <a href="default_files/Page520.htm">
           <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;
   line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;language:en-US">
            dd Personal History
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;
   language:en-US">
           ” link on the left of this page and fill in the simple form in your own words . Your information will be posted under “P
          </span>
          <a href="default_files/Page439.htm">
           <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;
   line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;language:en-US">
            ersonal Histories
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;
   language:en-US">
           ” and you will be added to the map.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
   125%;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           <span dir="ltr">
           </span>
           2. If you prefer not to post your personal history, just email us your name (first or last as you prefer), geographical location and where you are affected by melorheostosis to
          </span>
          <a href="mailto:map@melorheostosis.org?subject=map%20posting%20request">
           <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;
   text-decoration:underline;language:en-US">
            map@melorheostosis.org
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:125%;font-family:Arial;
   language:en-US">
           . This information will not be posted and your information will be kept confidential but you will be added to the map.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="MsoBodyText">
          <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
   125%;font-family:Arial;language:en-US">
           Let the medical community know you exist. Every ‘dot” on these maps represents a patient and a family facing the challenge of coping with melorheostosis. Stand up with them and be counted. We have strength in numbers none of us can possibly have alone. We look forward to hearing from you.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
    </span>

      <div dir="ltr">
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;text-align:center">
        <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:16.0pt;font-family:Arial;color:#CC0066;
   font-weight:bold;language:en-US">
         IMPORTANT  UPDATE FROM NIH
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal">
        <span lang="en-US" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;
   color:white;language:en-US">
         “On behalf of all the physicians and scientists working on Melorheostosis, thank you all for your participation in the ongoing research at NIH. You came out in masses when we asked for bone, skin, blood or really whatever it would take to make any progress. As a testimony to your patience and commitment, we are delighted to present to you our first milestone in understanding what causes Melorheostosis. We still have miles to go but we have made some progress.”
        </span>
       </p>
      </div>
